Accommodation: After all, the hotel has been built for a long time, so we can't be too picky. Guests with higher requirements are recommended to bring their own. The room has a low ceiling, which is completely different from modern hotels. It must have been a fashion in that era. The bed is quite comfortable. To sum up, although it is not up to the five-star level of new hotels now, it is still very good as an old hotel.
Marketing: Because we checked in on New Year's Eve, the hotel lobby layout and the behavior of the staff did not have a festive feeling. On the day we arrived on the 26th, the nucleic acid test done at 4 p.m. was reported at 00:08 on the 27th. After asking the front desk in the morning, we set off on our bike to do the nucleic acid test. Without thinking too much, we went back to the room, and then went downstairs to inquire.
